   [SaSū 1] evaṃ mayā śrutamekasmin samaye bhagavān rājagṛhe viharati sma /	[SaSU 1] evam mayA Srutam-ekasmin samaye BagavAn rAjagRhe viharati sma /

   [SaSū 2] dvāviṃśatibhirbhikṣusahasraiḥ tadyathā āyuṣmatā	[SaSU 2] dvAviMSatiBiH-Bikzu-sahasrEH tat-yaTA AyuzmatA
   cājñātakauṇḍinyena / āyuṣmatā ca mahāmaudgalyāyena / āyuṣmatā ca	ca-ajQAta-kONxinyena / AyuzmatA ca mahAmOdgalyAyena / AyuzmatA ca
   śāradvatīputreṇa / āyuṣmatā ca mahākāśyapena / āyuṣmatā ca rāhulena /	SAradvatI-putreNa / AyuzmatA ca mahAkASyapena / AyuzmatA ca rAhulena /
   āyuṣmatā ca bakkulena / āyuṣmatā ca bhadravāsena / āyuṣmatā ca bhadraśriyā	AyuzmatA ca bakkulena / AyuzmatA ca Badra-vAsena / AyuzmatA ca BadraSriyA
   / āyuṣmatā ca nandaśriyā / āyuṣmatā ca jāṅgulena / āyuṣmatā ca subhūtinā /	/ AyuzmatA ca nanda-SriyA / AyuzmatA ca jAFgulena / AyuzmatA ca suBUtinA /
   āyuṣmatā ca revatena / āyuṣmatā ca nandasenena / āyuṣmatā cānandena /	AyuzmatA ca revatena / AyuzmatA ca nandasenena / AyuzmatA ca-Anandena /
   evaṃpramukhairdvāviṃśatibhirbhikṣusahasraiḥ /	evaMpramuKEH-dvAviMSatiBiH-Bikzu-sahasrEH /
   [SaSū 3] dvāṣaṣṭibhiśca bodhisattvasahasraiḥ tadyathā maitreyeṇa ca	[SaSU 3] dvAzazwiBiH-ca boDisattva-sahasrEH tat-yaTA mEtreyeNa ca
   bodhisattvena mahāsattvena / sarvaśūreṇa ca bodhisattvena mahāsattvena /	boDisattvena mahAsattvena / sarva-SUreNa ca boDisattvena mahAsattvena /
   kumāraśriyā ca bodhisattvena mahāsattvena / kumāravāsinā ca bodhisattvena	kumAra-SriyA ca boDisattvena mahAsattvena / kumAra-vAsinA ca boDisattvena
   mahāsattvena / kumārabhadreṇa ca bodhisattvena mahāsattvena / anūnena ca	mahAsattvena / kumAraBadreNa ca boDisattvena mahAsattvena / anUnena ca
   (nāma) bodhisattvena mahāsattvena / maṃjuśriyā ca kumārabhūtena	(nAma) boDisattvena mahAsattvena / maMju-SriyA ca kumAra-BUtena
   bodhisattvena mahāsattvena / samantabhadrena ca bodhisattvena mahāsattvena	boDisattvena mahAsattvena / samantaBadrena ca boDisattvena mahAsattvena
   / sudarśanena ca bodhisattvena mahāsattvena / bhaiṣajyarājena ca	/ sudarSanena ca boDisattvena mahAsattvena / BEzajya-rAjena ca
   bodhisattvena mahāsattvena / (vajrasenena ca bodhisattvena mahāsattvena /)	boDisattvena mahAsattvena / (vajrasenena ca boDisattvena mahAsattvena /)
   evaṃpramukhairdvāṣaṣṭibhirbodhisattvasahasraiḥ	evaMpramuKEH-dvAzazwiBiH-boDisattva-sahasrEH
   [SaSū 4] dvāṣaṣṭibhiśca devaputrasahasraiḥ tadyathā arjunena ca	[SaSU 4] dvAzazwiBiH-ca deva-putra-sahasrEH tat-yaTA arjunena ca
   devaputreṇa / bhadreṇa ca devaputreṇa / subhadreṇa ca devaputreṇa /	deva-putreNa / BadreNa ca deva-putreNa / suBadreNa ca deva-putreNa /
   dharmarucinā ca devaputreṇa / candanagarbheṇa ca devaputreṇa / candavāsinā	Darma-rucinA ca deva-putreNa / candana-garBeNa ca deva-putreNa / canda-vAsinA
   ca devaputreṇa / candanena ca devaputreṇa / candanasenena ca devaputreṇa /	ca deva-putreNa / candanena ca deva-putreNa / candanasenena ca deva-putreNa /

   [SaSū 5] aṣṭābhiśca devakanyāsahasraiḥ tadyathā mṛdaṃginyā ca devakanyāyā	[SaSU 5] azwABiH-ca deva-kanyA-sahasrEH tat-yaTA mRdaMginyA ca deva-kanyAyA
   / prāsādavatyā ca devakanyāyā / mahātmasaṃprayuktayā ca devakanyāyā /	/ prAsAdavatyA ca deva-kanyAyAH / mahAtma-saMprayuktayA ca deva-kanyAyAH /
   varṣaśriyāyā ca devakanyāyā / (padmaśriyāya ca devakanyāyā /)	varza-SriyAyA ca deva-kanyAyAH / (padma-SriyAya ca deva-kanyAyAH /)
   prajāpativāsinyā ca devakanyāyā / balinyā ca devakanyāyā / subāhuyuktayā	prajApati-vAsinyA ca deva-kanyAyAH / balinyA ca deva-kanyAyAH / su-bAhu-yuktayA
   ca devakanyāyā / evaṃpramukhairaṣṭābhirdevakanyāsahasraiḥ	ca deva-kanyAyAH / evaMpramuKEH-azwABiH-deva-kanyA-sahasrEH
   [SaSū 6] aṣṭābhiśca nāgarājasahasraiḥ tadyathā apalālena ca nāgarājñā /	[SaSU 6] azwABiH-ca nAga-rAja-sahasrEH tat-yaTA apalAlena ca nAga-rAjQA /
   elapatreṇa ca nāgarājñā / timiṅgilena ca nāgarājñā / kuṃbhasāreṇa ca	ela-patreNa ca nAga-rAjQA / timiFgilena ca nAga-rAjQA / kuMBasAreNa ca
   nāgarājñā / kuṃbhaśīrṣeṇa ca nāgarājñā / sunandena ca nāgarājñā /	nAga-rAjQA / kuMBaSIrzeNa ca nAga-rAjQA / sunandena ca nAga-rAjQA /
   suśākhena ca nāgarājñā / gavaśīrṣeṇa ca nāgārājñā /	su-SAKena ca nAga-rAjQA / gavaSIrzeNa ca nAgArAjQA /
   evaṃpramukhairaṣṭābhirnāgarājasahasrais	evaMpramuKEH-azwABiH-nAga-rAja-sahasrEH-
   [SaSū 7] te sarve yena rājagṛhaṃ mahānagaraṃ yena gṛddhrakūṭaḥ parvato	[SaSU 7] te sarve yena rAjagRham mahA-nagaram yena gRdDrakUwaH parvataH-
   yena ca bhagavāṃcchākyamunistathāgato 'rhan	yena ca BagavAn=-CAkya-muniH-taTAgataH arhan
   samyaksaṃbuddhastenopasaṃkrāmadupasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau	samyaksaMbudDaH-tena-upasaMkrAmat-upasaMkramya BagavataH pAdO
   śirasābhivandya bhagavantaṃ triṣpradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavataḥ puratastasthire	SirasA-aBivandya Bagavantam trizpradakziNIkRtya BagavataH puratas-tasTire
   [SaSū 8] (etadavocan deśayatu bhagavāṃ dharmaṃ deśayatu sugataḥ dharmaṃ	[SaSU 8] (etat-avocan deSayatu BagavAm Darmam deSayatu sugataH Darmam
   yaṃ śrutvāsme kṣipramanuttarā samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhyema yena ca	yam SrutvA-asme kzipram-anuttarA samyaksaMboDim-aBisaMbudDyema yena ca
   sarvasattvānāṃ karmāvaraṇakṣayo bhaveyāt) bhagavāṃśca	sarva-sattvAnAm karma-AvaraNa-kzayaH Baveya-at) BagavAn=-ca
   tūṣṇībhāvenādhivāsayati sma /	tUzNIBAvena-aDivAsayati sma /
   [SaSū 9] atha khalu sarvaśūro bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ	[SaSU 9] aTa Kalu sarva-SUraH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH
   utthāyāsanādekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇaṃ jānumaṇḍalaṃ pṛthivyāṃ	utTAya-AsanAt-eka-aMsam-uttarAsaFgam kRtvA dakziNam jAnu-maNxalam pRTivyAm
   pratiṣṭhāpya yena bhagavāṃstenāṃjaliṃ praṇamayya bhagavantametadavocat	pratizWApya yena BagavAn=-tena-aMjalim praNamayya Bagavantam-etat-avocat-
   [SaSū 10] bahvyo bhagavan devakoṭyopsarakanyākoṭyo bodhisattvakoṭyaḥ	[SaSU 10] bahvyaH Bagavan deva-kowyA-upsara-kanyA-kowyaH boDisattva-kowyaH
   bahvyo bhagavaṃcchrāvakakoṭyaḥ sannipatitāḥ sanniṣaṇṇā dharmaśravaṇāya /	bahvyaH Bagavan=-SrAvaka-kowyaH sannipatitAH sannizaNNAH Darma-SravaNAya /
   tatsādhu bhagavan teṣāṃ yathāsannipatitānāṃ (sanniṣaṇṇānāṃ) tathāgato	tat-sADu Bagavan tezAm yaTA-sannipatitAnAm (sannizaNNAnAM) taTAgataH-
   'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhastathārūpaṃ dharmanayapraveśaṃ deśayatu / yathaiṣāṃ	arhan samyaksaMbudDaH-taTArUpam Darma-naya-praveSam deSayatu / yaTA-ezAm
   syāddīrgharātramarthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyānāṃ ca	syAt-dIrGarAtram-arTAya hitAya suKAya devAnAm ca manuzyAnAm ca
   yathārūpeṇa dharmanayapraveśena deśitena vṛddhānāṃ sattvānāṃ saha	yaTArUpeNa Darma-naya-praveSena deSitena vRdDAnAm sattvAnAm saha
   śravaṇenaiva sarvakarmāvaraṇāni caiṣāṃ parikṣayaṃ gaccheyuḥ daharāśca	SravaNena-eva sarva-karma-AvaraNAni ca-ezAm parikzayam gacCeyuH daharAH-ca
   sattvāḥ kuśaleṣu dharmeṣvabhiyujyamānā viśeṣāmadhigaccheyurna hīyeranna	sattvAH kuSalezu Darmezu-aBiyujyamAnAH viSezAm-aDigacCeyuH-na hIyeranna
   parihīyeran kuśalairdharmaiḥ //	parihIyeran kuSalEH-DarmEH //
   [SaSū 11] evamukte bhagavān sarvaśūraṃ bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvametadavocat	[SaSU 11] evam-ukte BagavAn sarva-SUram boDisattvam mahAsattvam-etat-avocat-

   tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhametamarthaṃ paripraṣṭavyaṃ manyase /	taTAgatam-arhantam samyaksaMbudDam-etam-arTam pariprazwavyam manyase /
   tena hi tvaṃ sarvaśūra śṛṇu sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasikuru.................	tena hi tvam sarva-SUra SRNu sADu ca suzWu ca manasikuru.................
   te /	te /
   [SaSū 12] evaṃ bhagavanniti sarvaśūro bodhisattvo mahāsattvo bhagavataḥ	[SaSU 12] evam Bagavan=-iti sarva-SUraH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH BagavataH

   [SaSū 13] bhagavan asyaitadavocat asti sarvaśūra [(saddharmaparyāyo / yena	[SaSU 13] Bagavan asya-etat-avocat asti sarva-SUraH [(sat-Darma-paryAyaH / yena
   dharmaparyāyeṇa sarvasatvānāṃ paṃcānantaryāṇi karmāvaraṇani kṣayaṃ	Darma-paryAyeNa sarva-satvAnAm paMcAnantaryANi karma-AvaraNani kzayam

   cānuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃbuddhayaṃteḥkataro bhagavaṃ	ca-anuttarAm samyaksaMboDim aBisaMbudDayaMteHkataraH Bagavam
   saddharmaparyāyaḥ	sadDarma-paryAyaH
   [SaSū 14] bhagavānāhaḥ) saṃghāṭo nāma dharmaparyāya / ya etarhi jambudvīpe	[SaSU 14] BagavAn-AhaH) saMGAwaH nAma Darma-paryAya / yaH etarhi jambudvIpe
   pracariṣyati / yaḥ kaścit sarvaśūremaṃ saṃghāṭaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śroṣyati /	pracarizyati / yaH kaScid sarva-SUra-imam saMGAwam Darma-paryAyam Srozyati /
   tasya pañcānantaryāṇi karmāṇi parikṣayaṃ yāsyanti / avaivartikāśca	tasya paQca-AnantaryANi karmANi parikzayam yAsyanti / avEvartikAH-ca
   bhaviṣyantyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau /	Bavizyanti-anuttarAyAm samyaksaMboDO /
   [SaSū 15] tatkiṃ manyase sarvaśūra ya imaṃ saṃghāṭasūtraṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ	[SaSU 15] tat-kim manyase sarva-SUra yaH imam saMGAwa-sUtram Darma-paryAyam
   śroṣyati / yathaikasya tathāgatasya [satkāraṃ kṛtvā] puṇyaskandhastathā	Srozyati / yaTA-ekasya taTAgatasya [satkAram kRtvA] puNya-skanDaH-taTA
   tāvantaṃ puṇyaskandhaḥ sa sattva prasaviṣyatīti / naivaṃ sarvaśūra	tAvantam puNya-skanDaH sa sattva prasavizyati-iti / na-evam sarva-SUra
   draṣṭavyaṃ /	drazwavyam /
   [SaSū 16] sarvaśūro bodhisattva āha / yathā kathaṃ punarbhagavan	[SaSU 16] sarva-SUraH boDisattvaH Aha / yaTA kaTam punar-Bagavan
   draṣṭavyaṃ /	drazwavyam /
   bhagavānāha / yathā gaṃgānadībālukāsamānāṃ tathāgatānāṃ arhatāṃ	BagavAn-Aha / yaTA gaMgA-nadI-bAlukA-samAnAm taTAgatAnAm arhatAm
   samyaksaṃbuddhānāṃ (satkāraṃ kṛtvā) puṇyaskandhastāvantaṃ sarvaśūra te	samyaksaMbudDAnAm (satkAram kRtvA) puNya-skanDaH-tAvantam sarva-SUra te
   satvāḥ puṇyaskandhaṃ prasaviṣyanti / ye sarvaśūra imaṃ saṃghāṭaṃ	satvAH puNya-skanDam prasavizyanti / ye sarva-SUraH imam saMGAwam
   dharmaparyāyaṃ śroṣyanti te sarve avaivartikā bhaviṣyanti (anuttarasyāṃ	Darma-paryAyam Srozyanti te sarve avEvartikAH Bavizyanti (anuttarasyAm
   samyaksaṃbodheḥ) / sarve ca tathāgataṃ drakṣyanti / sarve ca	samyaksaMboDeH) / sarve ca taTAgatam drakzyanti / sarve ca

   samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyante / adhṛṣyāśca bhaviṣyanti mārena pāpīmatā	samyaksaMboDim-aBisaMBotsyante / aDRzyAH-ca Bavizyanti mArena pApImatA
   / te ca sarve tadeva kuśaladharmamanuprāpsyanti / ye sarvaśūra imaṃ	/ te ca sarve tat-eva kuSala-Darmam-anuprApsyanti / ye sarva-SUraH imam
   saṃghāṭasūtraṃ śroṣyanti / te sarve utpādanirodhaṃ jñāsyanti /	saMGAwa-sUtram Srozyanti / te sarve utpAda-niroDam jQAsyanti /
   [SaSū 17] atha te sarve (yathāsannipatitā bodhisattvā mahāśrāvakā)	[SaSU 17] aTa te sarve (yaTA-sannipatitAH boDisattvAH mahA-SrAvakA)
   devanāgamanuṣyāpsarakanyākoṭyastena kālena tena samayenotthāyāsanebhyaḥ	deva-nAga-manuzya-apsara-kanyA-kowyaH-tena kAlena tena samayena-utTAya-AsaneByaH
   ekāṃsānyuttarāsaṃgāni kṛtvā dakṣiṇāni jānumaṇḍalāni pṛthivyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya	eka-aMsAni-uttarAsaMgAni kRtvA dakziNAni jAnu-maNxalAni pRTivyAm pratizWApya
   yena bhagavāṃstenāṃjalayaḥ praṇamayya (te sarve) bhagavantaṃ paripṛcchanti	yena BagavAn=-tena-aMjalayaH praNamayya (te sarve) Bagavantam paripRcCanti
   sma / kiyantaṃ bhagavannekasya tathāgatasya (satkāraṃ kṛtvā) puṇyaskandhaḥ	sma / kiyantam Bagavan=-ekasya taTAgatasya (satkAram kRtvA) puNya-skanDaH
   [SaSū 18] bhagavān āha / śṛṇu kulaputrā; ekasya buddhasya puṇyaskandhasya	[SaSU 18] BagavAn Aha / SRNu kula-putrA; ekasya budDasya puNya-skanDasya
   pramāṇaṃ tadyathā mahāsamudre udakabindavaḥ yāvanto jaṃbudvīpe paramāṇavaḥ	pramANam tat-yaTA mahA-samudre udaka-bindavaH yAvantaH jaMbudvIpe paramANavaH
   yathā gaṃgānadībālikāsamāḥ sattvāste sarve daśabhūmipratiṣṭhitā	yaTA gaMgA-nadI-bAlikA-samAH sattvAH-te sarve daSa-BUmi-pratizWitA
   bodhisattvā bhaveyuḥ yacca teṣāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ puṇyaskandhamato bahutaraṃ	boDisattvAH BaveyuH yat-ca tezAm boDisattvAnAm puNya-skanDam-atas bahutaram
   puṇyaskandhamekasya buddhasya (puṇyaskandham) / ataśca te sarvaśūra sattvā	puNya-skanDam-ekasya budDasya (puNya-skanDam) / atas-ca te sarva-SUra sattvA
   bahutaraṃ puṇyaskandhaṃ prasaviṣyanti ya imaṃ saṃghāṭaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ	bahutaram puNya-skanDam prasavizyanti yaH imam saMGAwam Darma-paryAyam
   śroṣyanti / yāvanna śakyaṃ gaṇanāyogena tasya puṇyaskandhasya	Srozyanti / yAvat-na Sakyam gaNanA-yogena tasya puNya-skanDasya
   paryantamadhigantuṃ / yasya sarvaśūra tasmin kāle tasmin samaye etad	paryantam-aDigantum / yasya sarva-SUra tasmin kAle tasmin samaye etat-
   vacanaṃ śrutvā mahānutsāho bhaviṣyati sa evamaprameyaṃ puṇyaskandhaṃ	vacanam SrutvA mahAn-utsAhaH Bavizyati saH evam-aprameyam puNya-skanDam
   prasaviṣyati /	prasavizyati /
   [SaSū 19] atha khalu sarvaśūro bodhisattvo mahāsattvo	[SaSU 19] aTa Kalu sarva-SUraH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH-

   bhaviṣyanti / evamukte bhagavān sarvaśūraṃ bodhisattvaṃ	Bavizyanti / evam-ukte BagavAn sarva-SUram boDisattvam
   mahāsattvametadavocat - dvāvimau sarvaśūra sattvau dharmaparitṛṣitau /	mahAsattvam-etat-avocat  dvO=-imO sarva-SUra sattvO Darma-paritRzitO /
   katamau dvau / yadutaikaḥ sarvaśūra sarvasattvasamacittaḥ dvitīyaḥ	katamO dvO / yat-uta-ekaH sarva-SUra sarva-sattva-sama-cittaH dvitIyaH
   sarvaśūra yo dharmaṃ śrutvā sarvasattvānāṃ samaṃ prakāśayati (imau dvau	sarva-SUra yaH Darmam SrutvA sarva-sattvAnAm samam prakASayati (imO dvO
   dharmaparitṛṣitau) /	Darma-paritRzitO) /
   [SaSū 20] sarvaśūro bodhisattva āha - katamaṃ bhagavan dharmaṃ śrutvā	[SaSU 20] sarva-SUraH boDisattvaH Aha  katamam Bagavan Darmam SrutvA
   sarvasattvānāṃ samaprakāśanā; bhagavān āha - ekaḥ sarvaśūra dharmaṃ śrutvā	sarva-sattvAnAm sama-prakASanA; BagavAn Aha  ekaH sarva-SUra Darmam SrutvA
   bodhāya pariṇāmayaṃti / yadā ca bodhāya pariṇāmayati tadā sarvasattvā	boDAya pariNAmayaMti / yadA ca boDAya pariNAmayati tadA sarva-sattvA
   dharmaparitṛṣitā bhaviṣyanti / dvitīyassarvaśūra yo mahāyānamavagāhayati	Darma-paritRzitAH Bavizyanti / dvitIyassarva-SUra yaH mahAyAnam-avagAhayati
   sa nityaṃ dharmaparitṛṣito bhavat /	sa nityam Darma-paritRzitaH Bavat /
   [SaSū 21] atha te devanāgamanuṣyāpsarasakoṭya utthāyāsanād bhagavataḥ	[SaSU 21] aTa te deva-nAga-manuzya-apsarasa-kowyaH utTAya-AsanAt BagavataH
   purataḥ prāṃjalayo bhūtvā bhagavantametadavocan vayaṃ bhagavan	puratas prAMjalayaH BUtvA Bagavantam-etat-avocan vayam Bagavan

   kulaputremānyanekāni gaṃgānadībālikāsamāni	kula-putra-imAni-anekAni gaMgA-nadI-bAlikA-samAni
   tathāgatakoṭīniyutaśatasahasrāṇi / āha / paśyāmi bhagavan paśyāmi sugata /	taTAgata-kowI-niyuta-Sata-sahasrANi / Aha / paSyAmi Bagavan paSyAmi sugataH /
   (bhagavān) āha / ete bhoḥ kulaputra tathāgatāstava sakāśamupasaṃkrāntā	(BagavAn) Aha / ete BoH kula-putra taTAgatAH-tava sakASam-upasaMkrAntA
   darśanāya / āha / kiṃ mayā kuśalakarma kṛtaṃ yeneme bahavastathāgatā āgatā	darSanAya / Aha / kim mayA kuSala-karma kRtam yena-ime bahavaH-taTAgatAH AgatA
   [SaSū 86] āha / śṛṇu kulaputra tvayā mānuṣyakamātmabhāvaṃ pratilabhya	[SaSU 86] Aha / SRNu kula-putra tvayA mAnuzyakam-Atma-BAvam pratilaBya
   saṃghāṭaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ śrotrāvabhāsamāgataṃ / tena tvayā etāvat	saMGAwam Darma-paryAyam Srotra-avaBAsam-Agatam / tena tvayA etAvat-
   puṇyaskandhaṃ prasūtaṃ / (sarvaśūra) āha / yadi mama bhagavanna etāvān	puNya-skanDam prasUtam / (sarva-SUra) Aha / yadi mama Bagavat-na etAvAn
   puṇyaskandhaḥ kaḥ punarvādo yaḥ sakalasamāptaṃ śroṣyati /	puNya-skanDaH kaH punar-vAdaH yaH sakala-samAptam Srozyati /
   [SaSū 87] (bhagavān) āhālaṃ bhoḥ kulaputra śṛṇu catuṣpadikāyā gāthāyā	[SaSU 87] (BagavAn) Aha-alam BoH kula-putra SRNu catuzpadikAyAH gATAyAH-
   (śrutāyāḥ) puṇyaṃ varṇayāmi / tadyathā kulaputra trayodaśa	(SrutAyAH) puNyam varNayAmi / tat-yaTA kula-putra trayodaSa
   gaṃgānadībālikāsamānāṃ tathāgatānāṃ arhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāṃ yaḥ	gaMgA-nadI-bAlikA-samAnAm taTAgatAnAm arhatAm samyaksaMbudDAnAm yaH
   puṇyasakandhastato bahutaraṃ puṇyaskandhaṃ prasavati / yaścatuṣpadikāmapi	puNya-sa-kanDaH-tatas bahutaram puNya-skanDam prasavati / yaH-catuzpadikAm-api

   yaścetaḥ saṃghāṭāddharmaparyāyādantaśaścatuṣpādikāmapi gāthāṃ śroṣyati /	yaH-ca-itaH saMGAwAt-Darma-paryAyAt-antaSas-catuzpAdikAm-api gATAm Srozyati /
   ayaṃ tato bahutaraṃ puṇyaskandhaṃ prasaviṣyati / kaḥ punarvādo yaḥ	ayam tatas bahutaram puNya-skanDam prasavizyati / kaH punar-vAdaH yaH
   sakalasamāptaṃ śroṣyati / na tasya puṇyaskandhasya śakyamupamāṃ kartum	sakala-samAptam Srozyati / na tasya puNya-skanDasya Sakyam-upamAm kartum
   [SaSū 88] śṛṇu kulaputra yaścemaṃ saṃghāṭaṃ (nāma) sūtraṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ	[SaSU 88] SRNu kula-putra yaH-ca-imam saMGAwam (nAma) sUtram Darma-paryAyam

   lokadhātau tilaṃ vāpayedyāvantaste tilaphalakāstāvanto rājānaścakravartino	lokaDAtO tilam vApayet-yAvantaH-te tila-PalakAH-tAvantaH rAjAnaH-cakravartinaH-

   āha / bahu bhagavan bahu sugata; bhagavān āha - yāvantaḥ kulaputra teṣāṃ	Aha / bahu Bagavan bahu sugata; BagavAn Aha  yAvantaH kula-putra tezAm
   rājñāṃ cakravartināṃ dānan dadataḥ puṇyaskandhaḥ yaścaikasya	rAjQAm cakravartinAm dAnan dadataH puNya-skanDaH yaH-ca-ekasya

   [SaSū 89] ye trisāhasramahāsāhasryāṃ lokadhātau sattvāste sarve srotaāpanā	[SaSU 89] ye tri-sAhasra-mahA-sAhasryAm lokaDAtO sattvAH-te sarve srotaApanA

   puṇyaskandhaḥ ayaṃ tato bahutaraṃ puṇyaskandhaṃ prasavati ya ekasya	puNya-skanDaH ayam tatas bahutaram puNya-skanDam prasavati yaH ekasya

   [SaSū 90] yaśca trisāhasramahāsāhasryāṃ lokadhātau tathāgataparipūrṇāyāṃ	[SaSU 90] yaH-ca tri-sAhasra-mahA-sAhasryAm lokaDAtO taTAgata-paripUrNAyAm

   kimaṃga punaḥ sarvaśūra ya iman dharmaparyāyaṃ śroṣyati / śrutvā ca	kim-aMga punar sarva-SUra yaH iman Darma-paryAyam Srozyati / SrutvA ca
   dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati parebhyaśca vistareṇa	DArayizyati vAcayizyati paryavApsyati pareByaH-ca vistareNa

   [SaSū 92] (bhagavān) āha / asti punaḥ sarvaśūra kaścit sattvo ya	[SaSU 92] (BagavAn) Aha / asti punar sarva-SUra kaScid sattvaH ya

   [SaSū 93] yena tathāgatakoṭīśatasahasrāṇi na dṛṣṭāni ta iman	[SaSU 93] yena taTAgata-kowI-Sata-sahasrANi na dRzwAni te iman

   [SaSū 96] śṛṇu sarvaśūra / punaraparaṃ guṇamāmantrayāmi / tadyathāpi	[SaSU 96] SRNu sarva-SUraH / punar-aparam guNam-AmantrayAmi / tat-yaTA-api

   tatra sattvaiḥ paribhāṣyate praharanti ca; kṣutpipāsārdito 'pi na	tatra sattvEH pariBAzyate praharanti ca; kzuD-pipAsA-arditaH api na

   [SaSū 98] sa kṣutpipāsāhetunā paribhāṣāhetunā prahārahetunā stūpabhedaṃ ca	[SaSU 98] sa kzuD-pipAsA-hetunA pariBAzA-hetunA prahAra-hetunA stu-upaBedam ca

   [SaSū 99] sa evaṃ cintayati gamiṣyāmyahaṃ parvatagirikandareṣu praviśāmi	[SaSU 99] saH evam cintayati gamizyAmi-aham parvata-giri-kandarezu praviSAmi
   tatra me kālakriyā bhaviṣyati na ca me iha kaści trātāsti / āha ca //	tatra me kAla-kriyA Bavizyati na ca me iha kaSci trAtA-asti / Aha ca //
   (20) kṛtaṃ me pāpakaṃ karma dagdhasthūnaṃ nirantaram	(20) kRtam me pApakam karma dagDa-sTUnam nirantaram

   (22) doṣahetoḥ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tena yāsyāmi durgatim	(22) doza-hetoH kRtam pApam tena yAsyAmi durgatim

   (107) nānāstaraṇaśayyābhiḥ kāyaḥ krīḍāpito mayā/	(107) nAnA-AstaraNa-SayyABiH kAyaH krIxA-pitaH mayA/

   (109) gandhavārṣikatailena sumanācaṇpakādibhiḥ	(109) ganDa-vArzika-tElena sumanA-caNpaka-AdiBiH

   (110) avatīrya hastipṛṣṭhādaśvapṛṣṭhe bhiruhya ca	(110) avatIrya hasti-pRzWAt-aSva-pRzWe Biruhya ca

   (115) kasmād vastraṃ pāṭayadhvaṃ pralāpaiścāpi kiṃkṛte /	(115) kasmAt vastram pAwayaDvam pralApEH-ca-api kiMkRte /

   (117) śarīraṃ me vṛkabhojyaṃ kurkurāṇāṃ ca vāyasām	(117) SarIram me vRka-Bojyam kurkurANAm ca vAyasAm

   (131) buddhānām sukhadaṃ kṣetraṃ dharmacakraṃ mahāgadam	(131) budDAnAm suKa-dam kzetram Darma-cakram mahA-gadam

   [SaSū 244] atha khalu bhagavān bhaiṣajyasenaṃ bodhisattvaṃ	[SaSU 244] aTa Kalu BagavAn BEzajya-senam boDisattvam

   [SaSū 245] atha khalu bhaiṣajyaseno bodhisattvo mahāsattvo	[SaSU 245] aTa Kalu BEzajyasenaH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH-

   [SaSū 246] atha te daharāḥ sattvā vyavalokya bhagavantametadavocan katame	[SaSU 246] aTa te daharAH sattvAH vyavalokya Bagavantam-etat-avocan katame

   [SaSū 247] atha te pūrvimakā sattvā daharāḥ ye prathamataramutpannāste	[SaSU 247] aTa te pUrvimakA sattvAH daharAH ye praTamataram-utpannAH-te

   [SaSū 248] atha khalu bhaiṣajyaseno bodhisattvo mahāsattvo	[SaSU 248] aTa Kalu BEzajyasenaH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH-
   ṛddhibalenotthāyāsanāt sārdhaṃ taiḥ paṃcabhirbodhisattvaśataiḥ te sarve	RdDi-balena-utTAya-AsanAt sArDam tEH paMcaBiH-boDisattva-SatEH te sarve
   ṛddhyā utthāyoparyantarīkṣe caṃkramanti / paryaṃkañca badhvā dhyāyanti /	RdDyAH utTAya-upari-antarIkze caMkramanti / paryaMkaQca baDvAH DyAyanti /
   teṣāṃ sarvakāyebhyaḥ siṃhā niṣkrāmanti / vyāghrā niṣkrāmanti / vyāḍā	tezAm sarva-kAyeByaH siMhAH nizkrAmanti / vyAGrAH nizkrAmanti / vyAxA

   [SaSū 249] atha khalu te daharāḥ sattvā bhagavantametadavocan - ko	[SaSU 249] aTa Kalu te daharAH sattvAH Bagavantam-etat-avocan  kaH-
   bhagavan hetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo mahāraśmyāvabhāsasya mahacca ṛddhivikurvitā	Bagavan hetuH kaH pratyayaH mahA-raSmyA-avaBAsasya mahat-ca RdDi-vikurvitA
   loke prādurbhūtāḥ bhagavān āha - paśyatha kulaputrā etau candrasūryau	loke prAdurBUtAH BagavAn Aha  paSyaTa kula-putrAH etO candra-sUryO
   prādurbhūtau / ta āhu / paśyāmo bhadanta bhagavan paśyāmo bhadanta sugata;	prAdurBUtO / te Ahu / paSyAmaH Badanta Bagavan paSyAmaH Badanta sugata;
   bhagavān āha - eṣa bodhisattvaiḥ svakāyād raśmyāvabhāso ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ	BagavAn Aha  eza boDisattvEH sva-kAyAt raSmyA-avaBAsaH RdDi-prAtihAryam
   ca darśitaṃ sandarśayitvā sattvānān dharman deśayanti / bahujanahitāya	ca darSitam sandarSayitvA sattvAnAn Darman deSayanti / bahu-jana-hitAya
   bahujanasukhāya lokānukaṃpāyairmahato janakāyasyārthāya hitāya sukhāya	bahu-jana-suKAya loka-anukaMpAyEH-mahataH jana-kAyasya-arTAya hitAya suKAya
   devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca ihaiva te mānuṣyake kāye vīryabalamupadarśayitvā	devAnAm ca manuzyANAm ca iha-eva te mAnuzyake kAye vIrya-balam-upadarSayitvA
   īdṛśam ṛddhibalamupadarśayanti / āha / deśayatu bhagavān	IdRSam RdDi-balam-upadarSayanti / Aha / deSayatu BagavAn
   raśmyāvabhāsaprādurbhāvāya dharmam	raSmyA-avaBAsa-prAdurBAvAya Darmam
   [SaSū 250] evamukte bhagavān bhaiṣajyasenaṃ bodhisattvaṃ	[SaSU 250] evam-ukte BagavAn BEzajya-senam boDisattvam
   mahāsattvametadavocat - paśyasi tvaṃ bhaiṣajyasena trisāhasramahāsāhasro	mahAsattvam-etat-avocat  paSyasi tvam BEzajyasena tri-sAhasra-mahA-sAhasraH-
   lokadhātuḥ ṣaḍvikāraṃ prakaṃpitaḥ āha / paśyāmi bhagavaṃ paśyāmi sugata /	lokaDAtuH zaz-vikAram prakaMpitaH Aha / paSyAmi Bagavam paSyAmi sugataH /
   tasya mama bhagavannevaṃ bhavatvahaṃ tathāgatametamarthaṃ paripṛccheyaṃ /	tasya mama Bagavan=-evam Bavatu-aham taTAgatam-etam-arTam paripRcCeyam /
   bhagavān āha - pṛccha tvaṃ bhaiṣajyasena yadyadevākāṃkṣasyahaṃ te tasya	BagavAn Aha  pRcCa tvam BEzajyasena yat-yat-eva-akAMkzasi-aham te tasya
   tasyaiva praśnasya vyākaraṇena cittamārādhayiṣyāmi nirdekṣyāmi	tasya-eva praSnasya vyAkaraNena cittam-ArADayizyAmi nirdekzyAmi
   vibhajiṣyāmi / bhaiṣajyasena yadatītānāgatapratyutpanneṣvadhvasu tatsarvaṃ	viBajizyAmi / BEzajyasena yat-atIta-anAgata-pratyutpannezu-aDvasu tat-sarvam
   darśayiṣyāmi / āha / deśayatu me bhagavan kaukṛtyavinodanārthaṃ / ihāhaṃ	darSayizyAmi / Aha / deSayatu me Bagavan kOkRtya-vinodana-arTam / iha-aham
   bhagavan paśyāmi tathāgataṃ caturaśītibhirdevaputrasahasraiḥ parivṛtaṃ	Bagavan paSyAmi taTAgatam caturaSItiBiH-deva-putra-sahasrEH parivRtam
   caturaśītibhiḥ koṭīsahasrairbodhisattvaiḥ parivṛtaṃ; dvādaśabhiḥ	caturaSItiBiH kowI-sahasrEH-boDisattvEH parivRtaM; dvAdaSaBiH

   caturdiśaṃ sa paśyati pūrvasyān diśi paṃcāśat koṭyo gaṃgānadīvālikāsamāni	caturdiSam sa paSyati pUrvasyAn diSi paMcASat kowyaH gaMgA-nadI-vAlikA-samAni
   bodhisattvānāmāgacchanti / dakṣiṇasyān diśi ṣaṣṭi koṭī	boDisattvAnAm-AgacCanti / dakziNasyAn diSi zazwi kowI
   gaṃgānadīvālikāsamāni bodhisattvānāmāgacchanti / paścimasyāṃn diśi saptati	gaMgA-nadI-vAlikA-samAni boDisattvAnAm-AgacCanti / paScimasyAM diSi saptati
   koṭī gaṃgānadīvālikāsamāni bodhisattvānāmāgacchanti / uttarasyān diśyaśīti	kowI gaMgA-nadI-vAlikA-samAni boDisattvAnAm-AgacCanti / uttarasyAn diSyaSIti
   koṭyo gaṃgānadīvālikāsamāni bodhisattvānāmāgacchanti / adhastāddiśi	kowyaH gaMgA-nadI-vAlikA-samAni boDisattvAnAm-AgacCanti / aDastAt-diSi
   navakoṭīsahasrāṇi gaṃgānadīvālikāsamāni bodhisattvānāmāgacchanti /	nava-kowI-sahasrANi gaMgA-nadI-vAlikA-samAni boDisattvAnAm-AgacCanti /
   ūrdhvāyāṃ diśi koṭīśatasahasraṃ gaṃgānadīvālikāsamāni	UrDvAyAm diSi kowI-Sata-sahasram gaMgA-nadI-vAlikA-samAni
   bodhisattvānāmāgacchanti / te cāgatāgatā bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhagavataḥ	boDisattvAnAm-AgacCanti / te ca-Agata-AgatAH boDisattvAH mahAsattvAH BagavataH
   purataḥ pādau śiraśābhivandyaikānte taśuḥ	puratas pAdO Sira-SA-aBi-vandya-ekAnte taSuH
   [SaSū 259] ekāntasthitānāṃ daśadigbhyāgatānāṃ bodhisattvānām	[SaSU 259] ekAnta-sTitAnAm daSa-diS-ByAgatAnAm boDisattvAnAm
   mahāsattvānāmatha bhaiṣajyaseno bodhisattvo mahāsattvo	mahAsattvAnAm-aTa BEzajyasenaH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH-
   bhagavantametadavocat - kimetad bhagavan khaga-m-antarīkṣe kṛṣṇarūpaṃ	Bagavantam-etat-avocat  kim-etat Bagavan Kaga-m-antarIkze kRzNa-rUpam
   lohitarūpaṃ (ca) paśyāmi / bhagavān āha - kimidaṃ bhaiṣajyasena / na	lohita-rUpam (ca) paSyAmi / BagavAn Aha  kim-idam BEzajyasena / na
   saṃjānāsi yadetadantarīkṣe kṛṣṇarūpaṃ lohitarūpaṃ ca paśyasi / āha / na	saMjAnAsi yat-etat-antarIkze kRzNa-rUpam lohita-rUpam ca paSyasi / Aha / na
   jānāmi bhagavan na jānāmi sugata / bhagavān āha - eṣa tathāgata eva jānāti	jAnAmi Bagavat na jAnAmi sugataH / BagavAn Aha  eza taTAgataH eva jAnAti
   / māro 'yaṃ bhaiṣajyasena vicakṣuskaraṇāyehopasaṃkrāntaḥ icchasi	/ mAraH ayam BEzajyasena vicakzuskaraNAya-iha-upasaMkrAntaH icCasi

   [SaSū 260] atha bhagavāṃstān bodhisattvān darśayitvā bhaiṣajyasenaṃ	[SaSU 260] aTa BagavAn=-tAn boDisattvAn darSayitvA BEzajya-senam
   bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvamāmantrayati sma / īdṛśānāṃ bhaiṣajyasena	boDisattvam mahAsattvam-Amantrayati sma / IdRSAnAm BEzajyasena
   koṭīśatagaṃgānadīvālikāsamāni bodhisattvānā āgatāni / āha / ko bhagavan	kowI-Sata-gaMgA-nadI-vAlikA-samAni boDisattvAnAH AgatAni / Aha / kaH Bagavan
   hetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo yadete bodhisattvā etāvanta ihāgatā / bhagavān āha -	hetuH kaH pratyayaH yat-ete boDisattvAH etAvantaH iha-AgatAH / BagavAn Aha -
   daharāṇāṃ sattvānāṃ pratyayena bhaiṣajyasena saṃprataṃ sarvasattvā	daharANAm sattvAnAm pratyayena BEzajyasena saMpratam sarva-sattvA
   dharmadhyānasamanvāgatā bhaviṣyanti / paśyasi tvaṃ bhaiṣajyasena ya ete	Darma-DyAna-samanvAgatAH Bavizyanti / paSyasi tvam BEzajyasena yaH ete
   bodhisattvā mahāsattvā nānārūpā āgatā ṛddhibalādhānena / āhāvalokitāni	boDisattvAH mahAsattvAH nAnA-rUpAH AgatAH RdDi-bala-ADAnena / Aha-avalokitAni
   mayā koṭīśatagaṃgānadīvālikāsamā lokadhātavastatra mayā	mayA kowI-Sata-gaMgA-nadIvAlikA-samA lokaDAtavaH-tatra mayA

   svakasvakena ṛddhibalena tiṣṭhanti nānārūpā nānāvarṇā	svaka-svakena RdDi-balena tizWanti nAnA-rUpA nAnA-varNA

   / dharmavihāreṣu te bodhisattvaparivārāstiṣṭhanti /	/ Darma-vihArezu te boDisattva-parivArAH-tizWanti /
   [SaSū 260] idamavocadbhagavān āttamanāḥ sarvaśuro bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ	[SaSU 260] idam-avocat-BagavAn Atta-manAH sarva-SuraH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH
